# PA ‚Üî vPA delta-log (flogence ‚Äî scrmlTS adaptation)

**Ratified S199 (2026-06-16); deputy-reframed S203 (2026-06-17).** The fine-grained PA‚Üídeputy absorption
stream. The deputy (the persistent vPA ‚Äî `vpa-scrml.md`) reads `[last-absorbed+1 .. now]` on a poke to
stay current WITHOUT re-reading the fat hand-off or cold-reading the docs. Append-only. Migrates into the
`flogence` repo when it's built; lives here now for the 2-manual-terminal immediate-benefit mode.

**Format:** one block per entry ‚Äî
```
[seq] kind  ¬∑ what-happened  ¬∑ ‚Üí pointer  ¬∑ (vpa: directive)
```
- **kind** ‚àà `rule` (user decision) ¬∑ `disp` (agent fired) ¬∑ `land` (commit landed) ¬∑ `find` (gap/bug/finding) ¬∑ `state` (board/test/sync delta) ¬∑ ~~`baton` (handoff)~~ (RETIRED S202 ‚Äî deputy model; historical entries S199 [17][18] / S200 [8][9] only). A deputy reboot-gap entry (Function 3, LIVE S203) is an ordinary `state` entry flagged `(deputy)`.
- **pointer** = SHA / file:line / gap-id / doc / agent-id (the vPA pulls detail only if needed)
- **(vpa: ‚Ä¶)** = optional; the ONLY field that asks the vPA to do/note something (hold ¬∑ sandbox a debate ¬∑ take ownership of agent X ¬∑ absorb-and-stand-by). Most entries omit it.

**Cadence:** the PA appends an entry at the moments it would write a hand-off bullet ‚Äî a ruling, a
dispatch, a landing, a finding, a state delta ‚Äî NOT per tool-call. The vPA absorbs the batch
since-last-poke at sparse checkpoints (prompt-cache TTL ‚Üí don't poke constantly; keep vPA context lean).

**Relationship to the other logs:** distinct from user-voice (verbatim user statements, durable) and
the changelog (per-session landings, coarse). This is the live PA-state stream the deputy absorbs; it does NOT
replace the wrap hand-off (kept for cold-start safety + audit) ‚Äî it replaces the deputy's *dependence* on it.

**Single-writer rule (refined S203):** only the LIVE PA appends to the source stream. The deputy is read-only
on this file ‚Äî the one narrow exception is the Function-3 (LIVE S203) reboot-gap entry (an ordinary `state` entry
flagged `(deputy)`, observation-only, recording an agent that landed while the PA was rebooting; never substantive).
